             style="display:block; width:100%; height:250px;"
             data-ad-client="ca-pub-6115205839762770"
             data-ad-slot="5247200044">

<script>
(function() {
    let adsLoaded = false;

    // 1. News items to rotate (Only the text changes, not the ad)
    const newsUpdates = [
        { text: "LIVE: Liverpool vs Real Madrid - Stats", link: "/match/1" },
        { text: "GOAL! Chelsea takes the lead - Live", link: "/match/2" },
        { text: "Top Match: Lakers vs Celtics - Preview", link: "/match/3" },
        { text: "Check Today's Full Schedule", link: "/schedule" }
    ];
    let newsIndex = 0;

    function startAnchor() {
        if (adsLoaded) return;
        adsLoaded = true;

        // 1. Show the UI structure immediately (but maybe keep it slightly transparent or off-screen if needed)
        // This ensures the div has a width (like 500px) when the script looks at it.
        const anchorEl = document.getElementById('manual-anchor');
        anchorEl.classList.add('show');

        // Load AdSense Script
        var s = document.createElement('script');
        s.async = true;
        s.src = "https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-YOUR_ID";
        s.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
        document.head.appendChild(s);

        s.onload = () => {
            // 2. THE FIX: Force a layout "reflow"
            // We ask for the width so the browser calculates the 100% or 500px right now.
            var forceReflow = anchorEl.offsetWidth;

            // 3. Load the ad now that width is guaranteed to be > 0
            try {
                (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("AdSense error:", e);
            }

            // Start ONLY the news rotation
            //setInterval(rotateNewsOnly, 15000);

            // Show close button after delay
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.getElementById('close-anchor').classList.add('visible');
            }, 5000);
        };
    }

    function rotateNewsOnly() {
        if (document.hidden) return;

        const tickerLink = document.getElementById('ticker-link');

        // Simple fade out/in effect for the news text
        tickerLink.style.opacity = 0;

        setTimeout(() => {
            newsIndex = (newsIndex + 1) % newsUpdates.length;
            tickerLink.innerText = newsUpdates[newsIndex].text;
            tickerLink.href = newsUpdates[newsIndex].link;
            tickerLink.style.opacity = 1;
        }, 500);
    }

    // Performance Triggers
    window.addEventListener('scroll', startAnchor, {once: true});
    window.addEventListener('touchstart', startAnchor, {once: true});
    setTimeout(startAnchor, 4000);
})();

//tooltip
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    const tooltip = document.getElementById("tooltip");
    let currentBadge = null;

    // Build a match map from hidden block
    const matchMap = {};
    document.querySelectorAll('#match-data [data-match]').forEach(div => {
        const id = div.dataset.match;
        matchMap[id] = { title: div.dataset.title, href: div.dataset.href };
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.form').forEach(badge => {

        // Hover tooltip
        badge.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
            const match = matchMap[badge.dataset.match];
            if(!match) return;

            tooltip.textContent = match.title;
            tooltip.style.display = 'block';
            const rect = badge.getBoundingClientRect();
            tooltip.style.top = (rect.top + window.scrollY - tooltip.offsetHeight - 8) + 'px';
            tooltip.style.left = (rect.left + window.scrollX + rect.width/2 - tooltip.offsetWidth/2) + 'px';
        });

        badge.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
            if(currentBadge !== badge) tooltip.style.display = 'none';
        });

        // Click badge: show tooltip only
        badge.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            const match = matchMap[badge.dataset.match];
            if(!match) return;

            if(currentBadge === badge){
                tooltip.style.display = 'none';
                currentBadge = null;
            } else {
                tooltip.textContent = match.title;
                const rect = badge.getBoundingClientRect();
                tooltip.style.top = (rect.top + window.scrollY - tooltip.offsetHeight - 8) + 'px';
                tooltip.style.left = (rect.left + window.scrollX + rect.width/2 - tooltip.offsetWidth/2) + 'px';
                tooltip.style.display = 'block';
                currentBadge = badge;

                // Tooltip click navigates
                tooltip.onclick = function() {
                    window.location.href = match.href;
                };
            }
        });
    });

    // Click outside closes tooltip
    document.addEventListener('click', function(){
        tooltip.style.display = 'none';
        currentBadge = null;
    });
});
</script>
